### ä¸­è¯(ä¸­è—¥) â†’ è¯(è—¥) â†’ æ¨‚(æ¨‚) â†’ ç™½(ç™½) â†’ çš‚(çš‚) â†’ æ—©(æ—©)

    - 'early'

### å²­å—(å¶ºå—) â†’ å²­(å¶º) â†’ é ˜(é ˜) â†’ é (é )
- **definition:** head
- **pinyin:** yÃ¨
- **components:**
  - é¦–
    - shÇ’u
    - head
  - å©
    - jiÃ©
    - kneeling person
- **etymology:**

## ä¸²ä¸²é¦™(ä¸²ä¸²é¦™)
---
## skewered hot pot
### chuÃ n chuÃ n xiÄng
---
- **definition:** skewered hot pot
- **pinyin:** chuÃ n chuÃ n xiÄng
- **components:**
  - ä¸²ä¸²
    - chuÃ nchuÃ n
    - skewers; skewered food
  - é¦™
    - xiÄng
    - fragrant; aromatic
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** ä¸²(ä¸²) (chuÃ n, "skewer") refers to food threaded on sticks, é¦™(é¦™) (xiÄng, "fragrant") describes the enticing aroma and flavor. Together, ä¸²ä¸² refers to the skewered items in hotpot, which are known for their fragrance.

    - In compound characters, the phonetic component determines the pronunciation.
